        <script type="text/javascript">
         $('.sticky').each(function()
			{
				var $elm = $(this);
				var $placeholder = $("<div class='placeholder'></div>");
				$placeholder.insertBefore($(this));

				$(window).resize(function()
				{
					if($elm.hasClass('fix-width'))
					{
						$elm.css('width', $placeholder.width());
					}
				}).trigger('resize');

				$(document).scroll(function()
				{
					if($(this).scrollTop() > $placeholder.offset().top)
					{
						if($elm.hasClass('fix-width'))
						{
							$elm.css('width', $elm.width());
						}

						$placeholder.css('height', $elm.innerHeight());

						$elm.addClass('fixed');

						if($elm.data('container'))
						{
							var end = $placeholder.parents($elm.data('container')).offset().top + $placeholder.parents($elm.data('container')).innerHeight();
							var margin = ($(document).scrollTop() + $elm.outerHeight(true)) - end;
							if(margin >= 1)
							{
								$elm.css('margin-top', (-1 * margin)+'px');
							}
						}
					}
					else
					{
						$placeholder.removeAttr('style');
						$elm.removeClass('fixed');

						if($elm.hasClass('fix-width'))
						{
							$elm.removeAttr('style');
						}
					}

			      	if($(this).scrollTop() > $placeholder.offset().top + $placeholder.height())
			        {
			          $elm.addClass('slim');
			        }
			        else
			        {
			          $elm.removeClass('slim');
			        }

				});
			});
        </script>

					var $menu = $(this).next('.menu');
	
					$menu.toggleClass('open');

               <div class="text">
                <h2>
                 <a href="http://everydaycarry.com/posts/29423/prometheus-preon-p1-mkiii-flashlight">
                  Prometheus Preon P1 MkIII Flashlight
                 </a>
                </h2>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 When you put together manufacturing prowess, over a decade of experience in pioneering flashlights, and the latest in flashlight tech, you're bound to get something special. And it's hard to describe the Preon P1 MkIII as anything but, with all the history behind it. Born out of the partnership of Prometheus Lights and Foursevens, the Preon represents a quality tool that only makers of their caliber can produce. Needless to say, it's one of the most refined AAA lights you can buy today.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 The
                 <a href="http://go.everydaycarry.com/plp1mk3" target="_blank">
                  Preon P1 MkIII's
                 </a>
                 exterior is a subtle fusion of both companies' design languages. On first glance you see the familiar Foursevens Preon, with its machined ridges and tapered middle barrel to accommodate your preferred grip method. Then there's the Prometheus screw-in titanium clip: a clip so good it sells on its own for other flashlights. Finally there's the materials the Preon comes in: Electroless Nickel plating and CR3 (Tri-Chrome) + PVD (Physical Vapor Deposition) coating over 6061-T6 aluminum, both technical solutions Prometheus have used to give their lights a unique total coating that doesn't mess with the light's rear click switch operation.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 In spite of its looks, the
                 <a href="http://go.everydaycarry.com/plp1mk3" target="_blank">
                  Preon P1 MkIII
                 </a>
                 isn't meant to be just pocket candy. It comes with the latest and greatest Nichia 219C LED, rated at 92+ CRI (Color Rendering Index) for the closest approximation to natural light you can currently get. It also allows for a higher current than its 219B predecessor, meaning it can more efficiently produce and hold its 100-lumen output. The Preon also comes with a programmable user interface, letting you pick from 6 configurations that make use of its 7 modes. An included NiMH AAA battery also gives the light a stable and rechargeable power source so you aren't wasting disposable batteries on your light (or harming it in the worst case).
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 While the Preon P1 MkIII marks the first steps of Prometheus and Foursevens, it's clear that the whole is greater than the sum of its parts and shows the clear influence and experience of both its creators. Learn more and pick one up for yourself in your choice of finish direct from Prometheus at the link below.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 <a class="btn-primary" href="http://go.everydaycarry.com/plp1mk3" target="_blank">
                  Check It Out
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>

               <div class="text">
                <h2>
                 <a href="http://everydaycarry.com/posts/29406/benchmade-486-saibu">
                  Benchmade 486 Saibu
                 </a>
                </h2>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 What makes for a good everyday carry knife? It's all in the details. And in the case of the new
                 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Benchmade-486-Saibu/dp/B07D9YG23Y/?tag=pd999-20" target="_blank">
                  Benchmade 486 Saibu
                 </a>
                 , it's chock full of 'em. Designed in collaboration with custom knifemaker Seiichi Nakamura, the Saibu not only offers an EDC-sized blade made of premium steel, but it also comes in a unique, attractive design that's built to stand up to your day-to-day. The name of the knife literally means "details," and they all come together in this decidedly modern gent's EDC folder.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 The
                 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Benchmade-486-Saibu/dp/B07D9YG23Y/?tag=pd999-20" target="_blank">
                  Saibu
                 </a>
                 features a premium CPM-20CV stainless steel drop point blade that's super sharp and wear resistant. At 2.98 it offers plenty of cutting edge for EDC tasks while keeping compact, making it an excellent option for EDCers in places with stricter knife laws. It's a plain edge knife with a high flat grind that lets it tackle slicing tasks with ease. But the curve at the tip lets you get in close for detail cutting work when needed.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 The Saibu also sports dual thumbstuds and Benchmade's AXIS lock, providing fully ambidextrous operation. That AXIS lock sits within a beautiful ergonomic handle made primarily of lightweight G10 scaling for superior grip and control. Windows are cut into the handle to save on weight, but also to add gorgeous cocobolo wood inlays, giving the Saibu a refined modern gent's look.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 But beyond the looks, the practicality of the design also means that this knife only weighs 2.7 ounces, making it barely noticeable in your pockets until you need to use it. The reversible tip-up deep carry pocket clip adds further versatility and convenience to carrying this stellar knife around everywhere.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 True to its name the Saibu is a detail-oriented modern gent's knife that has the design and the materials that make it an excellent choice for EDC. It's attractively-styled yet immensely practical, it's a knife that both looks great in hand and feels great when you actually have to use it. Check it out at the link below.
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 <a class="btn-primary" href="https://www.amazon.com/Benchmade-486-Saibu/dp/B07D9YG23Y/?tag=pd999-20" target="_blank">
                  View on Amazon
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
               <div class="short">
                <div class="credit">

                 </a>

               <div class="text">
                <h2>
                 <a href="http://everydaycarry.com/posts/29404/maker-knife">
                  Maker Knife
                 </a>
                </h2>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 "The Maker Knife is a sleek holder for utility blades. It features an adjustable and intuitive locking mechanism that kicks in when the blade reaches the top and automatically releases when..." (via
                 <a href="https://theawesomer.com/maker-knife/481777/" target="_blank">
                  TheAwesomer
                 </a>
                 )
                </p>
                <p class="abstract">
                 <a class="btn-primary" href="https://theawesomer.com/maker-knife/481777/" target="_blank">
                  Read More
                 </a>
                </p>

                  <i class="fa fa-chevron-right">
                  </i>

              </div>

            <script type="text/javascript">
             (function($) {
    var oldHide = $.fn.popover.Constructor.prototype.hide;

    $.fn.popover.Constructor.prototype.hide = function() {
        if (this.options.trigger === "hover" && this.tip().is(":hover")) {
            var that = this;
            // try again after what would have been the delay
            setTimeout(function() {
                return that.hide.call(that, arguments);
            }, that.options.delay.hide);
            return;
        }
        oldHide.call(this, arguments);
    };
})(jQuery);


var popover = false;
$(document).ready(function()
{
	var timeoutObj;
	$('.numbers [rel="popover"]').each(function()
	{
		var self = this;

		if($(this).data('title-only') == true)
		{
			var content = $("<div class='product-popover'><h3><a></a></h3></div>");
		}
		else
		{
			var content = $("<div class='flex-row product-popover'><div class='content'><h3><a></a></h3><div class='possessions'></div><div class='product-stats'></div><div class='popover-links'><a target='_blank' class='btn buy'>Purchase</a></div></div></div>");
			content.find('.btn.more').attr('href', $(this).data('url'));
			content.find('.btn.buy').attr('href', $(this).data('purchase'));
		
			if($(this).data('image')) {
				var $image = $("<div class='image'><img /></div>");
				$image.find('img').attr('src', $(this).data('image'));
				content.prepend($image);
			}

		}
		
		var product_name = $(this).data('product');
		
		content.find('h3 a').attr('href', $(this).data('url')).text(product_name);
		
		if($(this).data('discount'))
		{
			content.find('h3').append($("<span class='amzn-discount'><i class='fa fa-shopping-cart'></i> </span>").append($(this).data('discount')));
		}

		if($(this).data('possessions'))
		{
			content.find('.possessions').text($(this).data('possessions') + ($(this).data('possessions') == 1 ? " person has this" : " people have this"));
		}

/*
		if($(this).data('likes'))
		{
			content.find('.product-stats').append('<span class="favorites"><i class="fa fa-heart-o"></i> <span class="count">'+$(this).data('likes')+'</span></span>');
		}

		if($(this).data('comments'))
		{
			content.find('.product-stats').append('<span class="comments"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i> <span class="count">'+$(this).data('comments')+'</span></span>');
		}

		if($(this).data('views'))
		{
			content.find('.product-stats').append('<span class="views"><i class="fa fa-eye"></i> <span class="count">'+$(this).data('views')+'</span></span>');
		}
*/
		if(!content.find('.product-stats').children().length)
		{
			content.find('.product-stats').remove();
		}
		
		
		if($(this).data('product-id')) {
			content.find('a').each(function() {
				if($(this).attr('href') === $(self).data('purchase')) {
					$(this).attr('data-product-name', product_name);
					$(this).attr('data-track-product', $(self).data('product-id'));
				}
			});
		}
		
		
		var $elm = $(this);

		$elm.parents('.selection').on('click.popover', function()
		{
			$elm.popover('toggle');
		});

		$elm.popover({trigger: 'hover', delay: { hide: 100 }, html: true, 'content': $('<div></div>').append(content).html(), container: '#post-feed'}).on('show.bs.popover', function()
		{
			popover = this;
			setTimeout(function()
			{
				$(self).addClass('focused');

				var index = $(self).parents('.numbers').find(self).index()-1;
				$($(self).parents('.post').find('.details ol li').get(index)).addClass('focused hold').siblings('.focused:not(.hold)').removeClass('focused');
				$(self).parents('.numbers').addClass('preview');

				$(document).on("click.poppy", function(e)
				{
					if($(e.target).is(self) || $(e.target).parents('.popover').length)
					{
						return;
					}

					$elm.popover('hide');
				});
			}, 0);

		}).on('hide.bs.popover', function()
		{
			$(document).unbind("click.poppy");
			$(self).removeClass('focused hold');

			var index = $(self).parents('.numbers').find(self).index()-1;
			$($(self).parents('.post').find('.details ol li').get(index)).removeClass('focused hold');
			$(self).parents('.numbers').removeClass('preview');
			$(self).removeClass('focused hold');
		});
	});
});
            </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         $('#frontpage-sidebar').on('click', '.product a[href="#upvote"]', function(e)
			{
				e.preventDefault();

				var $product = $(this).parents('.product');

				if(!user)
				{
					return requireLogin();
				}
				
				$(this).toggleClass('active');
				var self = this;
				
				var action = $(this).hasClass('active') ? "add" : "remove";
				var validate = action == "add" ? "6d1ca3518b9a8d083147022c0fce15e3" : "70b3588cbec043b19a53ddbeb3ec4538";
				
				$.post(base_url + "favorites/"+action, { 'product': $product.data('id'), 'validate': validate}, function(result)
				{
					if(result.ok)
					{
						var number = parseInt($product.find('.clicks .number').text());
		
						if(action == 'add')
						{
							$product.find('.clicks .number').text(number + 1);
						}
						else
						{
							$product.find('.clicks .number').text(Math.max(number - 1, 0));
						}
					}
					else
					{
						$product.find('.clicks').toggleClass('active');
					}
				}, 'json');
			});
        </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       var timeout = false;
function homieLoaded()
{
console.log("home is loaded");

	$('.post-controller li.toggle.category').unbind('click').click(function()
	{
		$('#products-category-selector').appendTo('body').modal('show');
	});


	$('#post-feed .post').each(function()
	{
		var $post = $(this);
		$(this).imagesLoaded(function()
		{
			$post.trigger('redraw');
		}).progress(function(instance, img)
		{
			if(img.isLoaded)
			{
				$post.trigger('redraw');
			}
		}).always(function()
		{
			$post.trigger('redraw');
		});
	});

	$('#post-feed').unbind('click.thispage').on('click.thispage', '.post span.favorites', function()
	{
		console.log("clicked favorites", user);
		if(!user)
		{
			return requireLogin();
		}

		$(this).toggleClass('active');

		var self = this;


		var action = $(this).hasClass('active') ? "add" : "remove";
		var validate = action == "add" ? "6d1ca3518b9a8d083147022c0fce15e3" : "70b3588cbec043b19a53ddbeb3ec4538";

		$.post(base_url + "favorites/"+action, { 'post': $(this).parents('.post').data('id'), 'validate': validate}, function(result)
		{
			if(result.ok)
			{
				var number = parseInt($(self).find('.number').text());

				if(action == 'add')
				{
					$(self).find('.number').text(number + 1);
				}
				else
				{
					$(self).find('.number').text(Math.max(number - 1, 0));
				}
			}
			else
			{
				$(self).toggleClass('active');
			}
		}, 'json');
	});



	$('#post-feed').on('mouseover', '.numbers .selection', function()
	{
		var index = $(this).parents('.numbers').find(this).index()-1;
		$($(this).parents('.post').find('.details ol li').get(index)).addClass('focused').siblings('.focused:not(.hold)').removeClass('focused');
	}).on('mouseout', '.numbers .selection', function()
	{
		if($(this).hasClass('hold')) { return; }
		$(this).parents('.post').find('.details ol li:not(.hold)').removeClass('focused');
	});

		$('#post-feed').on('mouseover', '.details ol li', function()
	{
		var index = $(this).parents('ol').find(this).index();
		$($(this).parents('.post').find('.numbers .selection').get(index)).addClass('focused').siblings('.focused:not(.hold)').removeClass('focused');

		$(this).parents('.post').find('.numbers').addClass('preview');
	}).on('mouseout', '.details ol li', function()
	{
		if($(this).hasClass('hold')) { return; }
		$(this).parents('.post').find('.numbers .selection:not(.hold)').removeClass('focused');
		$(this).parents('.post').find('.numbers').removeClass('preview');
	});

	

	$('#post-feed').on('click', '.numbers .selection', function()
	{
		var index = $(this).parents('.numbers').find(this).index() - 1;

		$(this).toggleClass('focused hold');
		$($(this).parents('.post').find('.details ol li').get(index)).toggleClass('focused hold');
		if($($(this).parents('.post').find('.details ol li').get(index)).hasClass('hold'))
		{
			$($(this).parents('.post').find('.details ol li').get(index)).addClass('focused');
		}
	});

	$('#post-feed').on('click', '.share-it', function(e)
	{
		e.preventDefault();

		var $post = $(this).parents('.post');

		if($(this).attr('href') == '#twitter')
		{
			twShare(($post.data('url')), ($post.data('title')), 520, 350);
		}
		else if($(this).attr('href') == '#retweet')
		{
			twRetweet(($post.data('tw-share-id')), 520, 350);
		}
		else if($(this).attr('href') == '#facebook')
		{
			fbShare(encodeURIComponent($post.data('url')), encodeURIComponent($post.data('title')), encodeURIComponent($post.data('summary')), encodeURIComponent($post.data('image')), 520, 350);
		}
		else if($(this).attr('href') == '#fbembed')
		{
			fbEmbed(($post.data('fb-share-id')), 600, 600);
		}
	});

}




$('#post-feed').on('load', '.post', function()
{
	$(this).trigger('redraw');
});

$('#post-feed .post').each(function()
{
	$(this).find('.items').each(function()
	{
		var $items = $(this);
		var items = $(this).find('li').length;
		
		if(items > 10)
		{
			$(this).addClass('max10');
			
			if($(this).find('li:visible').length == 10)
			{
				var $truncated = $("<li class='truncated'>and "+(items-10)+" more</li>");
				$truncated.click(function()
				{
					$items.removeClass('max10');
					$truncated.remove();
				});
				
				$(this).append($truncated);
			}
		}
	});
});

var shrink_timeout = false;
$(window).unbind('resize.postlength').bind('resize.postlength', function()
{
	window.clearTimeout(shrink_timeout);
	shrink_timeout = window.setTimeout(function()
	{
		$('#post-feed .post').trigger('redraw');
	}, 200);
}).trigger('resize');


$('.post .numbers').each(function()
{
	var pos = [];
	
	var $numbers = $(this);
	
	$(this).find('.selection').each(function()
	{
		var $selection = $(this);
			
		$(this).bind('mousemove.thispage', function(e)
		{
			var $selected = $(this);
			
			$numbers.find('.selection').each(function()
			{
				
				if($(this).is($selected))
				{
					return;
				}
				
				var coords = [$(this).offset().left, $(this).offset().top, $(this).offset().left + $(this).outerWidth(true), $(this).offset().top + $(this).outerHeight(true)];
				
				var margin = 10;
				if($(this).offset().left > $selected.offset().left - margin && $(this).offset().left + $(this).outerWidth(true) < $selected.offset().left + $selected.outerWidth(true) + margin && $(this).offset().top > $selected.offset().top - margin  && $(this).offset().top + $(this).outerHeight(true) < $selected.offset().top + $selected.outerHeight(true) + margin)
				{
					$(this).css('z-index', 10);
				}
				
				
			});
			
		});
	});
});


$('#post-feed').imagesLoaded(function()
{
	$(window).trigger('resize');

}).progress(function(instance, img)
{
	if(img.isLoaded)
	{
		window.clearTimeout(timeout);
		timeout = window.setTimeout(function()
		{
			$(window).trigger('resize');
		}, 50);
	}
}).always(function()
{
	$(window).trigger('resize');
});

homieLoaded();
      </script>

   $('#signon-modal #social-login .twitter').unbind('click').click(function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
		
		if(typeof ga != 'undefined')
		{
			ga('send', "event", 'Sign On', 'Click', 'Twitter');
		}
		
		var pop = popup($(this).attr('href')+"?display=frame", { width: 700, height: 600}, function()
		{
			window.location.href = base_url + "login/twitter?signon-pop=1";
		});
	});

	$('#signon-modal #social-login .facebook').unbind('click').click(function(e)
	{
		e.preventDefault();
		
		if(typeof ga != 'undefined')
		{
			ga('send', "event", 'Sign On', 'Click', 'Facebook');
		}
		
		FB.login(function(result)
		{
			window.location.href = base_url + "login/facebook?signon-pop=1";
		}, {scope: 'public_profile,email,user_birthday,user_location,user_friends'});
	});	
	
	$('#signon-modal input').change(function()
	{
		if(typeof ga != 'undefined')
		{
			ga('send', "event", 'Sign On', 'Input', $(this).attr('name').toUpperCase());
		}
	});
	
	$('#signon-modal form').submit(function()
	{
		if(typeof ga != 'undefined')
		{
			ga('send', "event", 'Sign On', 'Submit', "Native");
		}
	});

      safari_web_id: "web.onesignal.auto.44e6ca0d-bbca-461f-908e-69d9a6be2a2a",
      autoRegister: false, /* Set to true to automatically prompt visitors */
      httpPermissionRequest: {
        enable: true
      },
      notifyButton: {
        /* Your other notify button settings here ... */
        enable: true,
        displayPredicate: function() {
            return OneSignal.isPushNotificationsEnabled()
                .then(function(isPushEnabled) {
	                isPushSubscribed = isPushEnabled;
                    /* The user is subscribed, so we want to return "false" to hide the notify button */
                    return !isPushEnabled;
                });
        },
	  },
	  promptOptions: {

    OneSignal.push(function() {
		OneSignal.setDefaultNotificationUrl("http:\/\/everydaycarry.com\/");
		OneSignal.setDefaultTitle("Everyday Carry - What are your EDC essentials?");
		OneSignal.on('subscriptionChange', function (isSubscribed) {
			isPushSubscribed = isSubscribed;
			if(typeof confetti !== 'undefined') {
				confetti(isSubscribed);
			}
		});
		
		setTimeout(function() {
			if (!isPushSubscribed) {
				  OneSignal.showHttpPermissionRequest();
			}
		}, 10 * 1000);
	});
